         Regex for password must contain at least eight characters, at least one number and both lower and uppercase letters and special characters
        </a>
       </h1>
       <div class="ml12 aside-cta flex--item print:d-none sm:ml0 sm:mb12 sm:order-first sm:as-end">

          <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
           <p>
            I want a regular expression to check that:
           </p>
           <p>
            A password contains at least eight characters, including at least one number and  includes both lower and uppercase letters and special characters, for example
            <code>
             #
            </code>
            ,
            <code>
             ?
            </code>
            ,
            <code>
             !
            </code>
            .
           </p>
           <p>
            It cannot be your old password or contain your username,
            <code>
             "password"
            </code>
            , or
            <code>
             "websitename"
            </code>
           </p>
           <p>
            And here is my validation expression which is for eight characters including one uppercase letter, one lowercase letter, and one number or special character.
           </p>
           <pre><code>(?=^.{8,}$)((?=.*\d)|(?=.*\W+))(?![.\n])(?=.*[A-Z])(?=.*[a-z]).*$"
</code></pre>
           <p>
            How can I write it for
            <strong>
             a password must be eight characters including one uppercase letter, one special character and alphanumeric characters
            </strong>
            ?
           </p>
          </div>
          <div class="mt24 mb12">
           <div class="post-taglist d-flex gs4 gsy fd-column">
            <div class="d-flex ps-relative fw-wrap">

        </a>
        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="21456918" data-highest-scored="1" data-parentid="19605150" data-position-on-page="1" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="0" data-score="1836" id="answer-21456918" itemprop="acceptedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="21456918">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="1836" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             1836
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/21456918/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Minimum eight characters, at least one letter and one number:
            </p>
            <pre><code>"^(?=.*[A-Za-z])(?=.*\d)[A-Za-z\d]{8,}$"
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Minimum eight characters, at least one letter, one number and one special character:
            </p>
            <pre><code>"^(?=.*[A-Za-z])(?=.*\d)(?=.*[@$!%*#?&amp;])[A-Za-z\d@$!%*#?&amp;]{8,}$"
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Minimum eight characters, at least one uppercase letter, one lowercase letter and one number:
            </p>
            <pre><code>"^(?=.*[a-z])(?=.*[A-Z])(?=.*\d)[a-zA-Z\d]{8,}$"
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Minimum eight characters, at least one uppercase letter, one lowercase letter, one number and one special character:
            </p>
            <pre><code>"^(?=.*[a-z])(?=.*[A-Z])(?=.*\d)(?=.*[@$!%*?&amp;])[A-Za-z\d@$!%*?&amp;]{8,}$"
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Minimum eight and maximum 10 characters, at least one uppercase letter, one lowercase letter, one number and one special character:
            </p>
            <pre><code>"^(?=.*[a-z])(?=.*[A-Z])(?=.*\d)(?=.*[@$!%*?&amp;])[A-Za-z\d@$!%*?&amp;]{8,10}$"
</code></pre>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">
            <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">
             <time datetime="2014-01-30T12:44:17" itemprop="dateCreated">

              <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 "^(?=.*[A-Za-z])(?=.*\d)[A-Za-z\d]{8,}$" does not allow symbols as one of the 8 characters
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">
                 –
                 <a class="comment-user" href="/users/1123777/wee" title="278 reputation">
                  Wee
                 </a>
                </div>
                <span class="comment-date" dir="ltr">

                 </span>

               </div>

             </li>
             <li class="comment js-comment" data-comment-id="110073014" data-comment-owner-id="2548928" data-comment-score="28" id="comment-110073014">
              <div class="js-comment-actions comment-actions">
               <div class="comment-score js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="hot" title="number of 'useful comment' votes received">
                 28
                </span>
               </div>
              </div>
              <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 I found the following allowed for all characters (special &amp; punctuation), without making them mandatory: "^(?=.*[a-z])(?=.*[A-Z])(?=.*\d)[a-zA-Z\d\w\W]{8,}$"
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">
                 –
                 <a class="comment-user" href="/users/2548928/gavin" title="113 reputation">
                  Gavin
                 </a>
                </div>
                <span class="comment-date" dir="ltr">

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="19605207" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="19605150" data-position-on-page="2" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="0" data-score="645" id="answer-19605207" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="19605207">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="645" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             645
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/19605207/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             You may use this regex with multiple
             <a href="https://www.regular-expressions.info/lookaround.html" rel="noreferrer">
              lookahead assertions (conditions)
             </a>
             :
            </p>
            <pre><code>^(?=.*?[A-Z])(?=.*?[a-z])(?=.*?[0-9])(?=.*?[#?!@$%^&amp;*-]).{8,}$
</code></pre>
            <p>
             This regex will enforce these rules:
            </p>
            <ul>
             <li>
              At least one upper case
              <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_alphabet" rel="noreferrer">
               English letter
              </a>
              ,
              <code>
               (?=.*?[A-Z])
              </code>
             </li>
             <li>
              At least one lower case English letter,
              <code>
               (?=.*?[a-z])
              </code>
             </li>
             <li>
              At least one digit,
              <code>
               (?=.*?[0-9])
              </code>
             </li>
             <li>
              At least one special character,
              <code>
               (?=.*?[#?!@$%^&amp;*-])
              </code>
             </li>
             <li>
              Minimum eight in length
              <code>
               .{8,}
              </code>
              (with the anchors)
             </li>
            </ul>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">

        <a name="33589907">
        </a>
        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="33589907" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="19605150" data-position-on-page="3" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="0" data-score="99" id="answer-33589907" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="33589907">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="99" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             99
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/33589907/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Regular expressions don't have an AND operator, so it's pretty hard to write a regex that matches valid passwords, when validity is defined by something AND something else AND something else...
            </p>
            <p>
             But, regular expressions do have an OR operator, so just apply DeMorgan's theorem, and write a regex that matches invalid passwords:
            </p>
            <p>
             Anything with less than eight characters
             <strong>
              OR
             </strong>
             anything with no numbers
             <strong>
              OR
             </strong>
             anything with no uppercase
             <strong>
              OR
             </strong>
             or anything with no lowercase
             <strong>
              OR
             </strong>
             anything with no special characters.
            </p>
            <p>
             So:
            </p>
            <pre><code>^(.{0,7}|[^0-9]*|[^A-Z]*|[^a-z]*|[a-zA-Z0-9]*)$
</code></pre>
            <p>
             If anything matches that, then it's an invalid password.
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">
            <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">
             <time datetime="2015-11-08T01:56:39" itemprop="dateCreated">
             </time>
             <div class="flex--item mr16" style="flex: 1 1 100px;">
              <div class="js-post-menu pt2" data-post-id="33589907">
               <div class="d-flex gs8 s-anchors s-anchors__muted fw-wrap">

                 Okay, I was afraid you were one of those computer scientists we sometimes get who don't realize there's a difference between
                 <i>
                  regular expressions
                 </i>
                 and
                 <i>
                  regexes
                 </i>
                 . ;)  It's true that many regex tasks are much simpler if you can negate the match result afterward, but that isn't always possible.  That's a beautiful regex, though.  It's not simple, it's elegant!
                </span>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="21052485" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="19605150" data-position-on-page="4" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="0" data-score="46" id="answer-21052485" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="21052485">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="46" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             46
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/21052485/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Just a small improvement for @anubhava's answer: Since special character are limited to the ones in the keyboard, use this for any special character:
            </p>
            <p>
             <code>
              ^(?=.*?[A-Z])(?=(.*[a-z]){1,})(?=(.*[\d]){1,})(?=(.*[\W]){1,})(?!.*\s).{8,}$
             </code>
            </p>
            <p>
             This regex will enforce these rules:
            </p>
            <ul>
             <li>
              At least one upper case English letter
             </li>
             <li>
              At least one lower case English letter
             </li>
             <li>
              At least one digit
             </li>
             <li>
              At least one special character
             </li>
             <li>
              Minimum eight in length
             </li>
            </ul>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">

               </div>
              </div>
              <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 In the JavaScript flavor,
                 <code>
                  \W
                 </code>
                 matches only ASCII characters.  So you haven't changed that, and now you have to filter out whitespace characters.  Furthermore, all the parentheses and
                 <code>
                  {1,}
                 </code>
                 quantifiers you added are pure noise, and removing the non-greedy (
                 <code>
                  ?
                 </code>
                 ) operators was pointless.  There is no improvement here.
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">
                 –
                 <a class="comment-user" href="/users/20938/alan-moore" title="71,119 reputation">
                  Alan Moore
                 </a>
                </div>
                <span class="comment-date" dir="ltr">
                 <span class="relativetime-clean" title="2015-11-08 06:00:43Z, License: CC BY-SA 3.0">
                  Nov 8, 2015 at 6:00
                 </span>
                </span>
               </div>
              </div>
             </li>
             <li class="comment js-comment" data-comment-id="88744142" data-comment-owner-id="5291014" data-comment-score="0" id="comment-88744142">
              <div class="js-comment-actions comment-actions">
               <div class="comment-score js-comment-edit-hide">
               </div>
              </div>
              <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 And How to avoid for empty string. Empty string regex should return true.   I have used following regex (?=.*[0-9])(?=.*[a-z])(?=.*[A-Z])(?=.*[@#$%^&amp;+=])(?=\\S+$).{8,15}
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">
                 –
                 <a class="comment-user" href="/users/5291014/coder" title="390 reputation">
                  Coder
                 </a>
                </div>
                <span class="comment-date" dir="ltr">
                 <span class="relativetime-clean" title="2018-06-15 07:52:25Z, License: CC BY-SA 4.0">
                  Jun 15, 2018 at 7:52
                 </span>
                </span>
               </div>
              </div>
             </li>
             <li class="comment js-comment" data-comment-id="100837332" data-comment-owner-id="7906671" data-comment-score="3" id="comment-100837332">
              <div class="js-comment-actions comment-actions">
               <div class="comment-score js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="cool" title="number of 'useful comment' votes received">
                 3
                </span>
               </div>
              </div>
              <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 fails for _ special character
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">
                 –
                 <a class="comment-user" href="/users/7906671/akhilesh" title="475 reputation">
                  Akhilesh
                 </a>
                </div>
                <span class="comment-date" dir="ltr">
                 <span class="relativetime-clean" title="2019-07-23 10:10:48Z, License: CC BY-SA 4.0">
                  Jul 23, 2019 at 10:10
                 </span>
                </span>
               </div>
              </div>
             </li>
             <li class="comment js-comment" data-comment-id="115861419" data-comment-owner-id="5527985" data-comment-score="0" id="comment-115861419">
              <div class="js-comment-actions comment-actions">
               <div class="comment-score js-comment-edit-hide">
               </div>
              </div>
              <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 To consider the underscore a
                 <i>
                  special character
                 </i>
                 as well and some further other improvements, try eg:
                 <a href="https://regex101.com/r/5UQT7f/1/" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
                  <code>
                   ^(?=[^A-Z\s]*[A-Z])(?=[^a-z\s]*[a-z])(?=[^\d\s]*\d)(?=\w*[\W_])\S{8,}$
                  </code>
                 </a>
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">
                 –
                 <a class="comment-user" href="/users/5527985/bobble-bubble" title="11,504 reputation">
                  bobble bubble
                 </a>
                </div>
                <span class="comment-date" dir="ltr">

                  Jan 1, 2021 at 19:46
                 </span>
                </span>
               </div>

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="45080884">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

            </div>

              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>

            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/45080884/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Use the following Regex to satisfy the below conditions:
            </p>
            <p>
             Conditions:
            </p>
            <ol>
             <li>
              Min 1 uppercase letter.
             </li>
             <li>
              Min 1 lowercase letter.
             </li>
             <li>
              Min 1 special character.
             </li>
             <li>
              Min 1 number.
             </li>
             <li>
              Min 8 characters.
             </li>
             <li>
              Max 30 characters.
             </li>
            </ol>
            <p>
             Regex:
            </p>
            <pre class="lang-regex prettyprint-override"><code>/^(?=.*[a-z])(?=.*[A-Z])(?=.*\d)(?=.*[#$@!%&amp;*?])[A-Za-z\d#$@!%&amp;*?]{8,30}$/
</code></pre>
           </div>

        <a name="33292812">
        </a>
        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="33292812" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="19605150" data-position-on-page="6" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="0" data-score="38" id="answer-33292812" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="33292812">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="38" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             38
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/33292812/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             I had some difficulty following the most popular answer for my circumstances. For example, my validation was failing with characters such as
             <code>
              ;
             </code>
             or
             <code>
              [
             </code>
             . I was not interested in white-listing my special characters, so I instead leveraged
             <code>
              [^\w\s]
             </code>
             as a test - simply put - match non word characters (including numeric) and non white space characters. To summarize, here is what worked for me...
            </p>
            <ul>
             <li>
              at least
              <code>
               8
              </code>
              characters
             </li>
             <li>
              at least
              <code>
               1
              </code>
              numeric character
             </li>
             <li>
              at least
              <code>
               1
              </code>
              lowercase letter
             </li>
             <li>
              at least
              <code>
               1
              </code>
              uppercase letter
             </li>
             <li>
              at least
              <code>
               1
              </code>
              special character
             </li>
            </ul>
            <hr/>
            <pre><code>/^(?=.*?[A-Z])(?=.*?[a-z])(?=.*?[0-9])(?=.*?[^\w\s]).{8,}$/
</code></pre>
            <p>
             <a href="http://jsfiddle.net/2bv9zn0y/">
              JSFiddle Link
             </a>
             - simple demo covering various cases
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">
            <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">
             <time datetime="2015-10-23T00:05:03" itemprop="dateCreated">
             </time>

               <div class="d-flex gs8 s-anchors s-anchors__muted fw-wrap">

              <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 I really like this answer except that it can't accept underscores. All I did was replace
                 <code>
                  (?=.*?[^\w\s])
                 </code>
                 with
                 <code>
                  (?=.*?([^\w\s]|[_]))
                 </code>
                 to add support for underscores and it works great now.   Also @Dinish.net the system I use trims the whitespace out of the password string when we get it, so using vanilla JS
                 <a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/String/Trim" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
                  String.prototype.trim()
                 </a>
                 method would work well if you want to use this answer.
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">
                 –
                 <a class="comment-user" href="/users/4322062/devin-carpenter" title="855 reputation">
                  Devin Carpenter

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             A more "generic" version(?), allowing none English letters as
             <em>
              special characters
             </em>
             .
            </p>
            <pre><code>^(?=\S*[a-z])(?=\S*[A-Z])(?=\S*\d)(?=\S*[^\w\s])\S{8,}$
</code></pre>
            <p>
             <div class="snippet" data-babel="false" data-console="true" data-hide="false" data-lang="js">
              <div class="snippet-code">
               <pre class="snippet-code-js lang-js prettyprint-override"><code>var pwdList = [
    '@@V4-\3Z`zTzM{&gt;k',
    '12qw!"QW12',
    '123qweASD!"#',
    '1qA!"#$%&amp;',
    'Günther32',
    '123456789',
    'qweASD123',
    'qweqQWEQWEqw',
    '12qwAS!'
  ],
  re = /^(?=\S*[a-z])(?=\S*[A-Z])(?=\S*\d)(?=\S*[^\w\s])\S{8,}$/;
  
  pwdList.forEach(function (pw) {
    document.write('&lt;span style="color:'+ (re.test(pw) ? 'green':'red') + '"&gt;' + pw + '&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br/&gt;');
  });</code></pre>
              </div>
             </div>
            </p>
           </div>

        <a name="49721224">
        </a>
        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="49721224" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="19605150" data-position-on-page="8" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="0" data-score="19" id="answer-49721224" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="49721224">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="19" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             19
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/49721224/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             I would reply to Peter Mortensen, but I don't have enough reputation.
            </p>
            <p>
             His expressions are perfect for each of the specified minimum requirements. The problem with his expressions that don't require special characters is that they also don't ALLOW special characters, so they also enforce maximum requirements, which I don't believe the OP requested. Normally you want to allow your users to make their password as strong as they want; why restrict strong passwords?
            </p>
            <p>
             So, his "minimum eight characters, at least one letter and one number" expression:
            </p>
            <p>
             <code>
              ^(?=.*[A-Za-z])(?=.*\d)[A-Za-z\d]{8,}$
             </code>
            </p>
            <p>
             achieves the minimum requirement, but the remaining characters can
             <em>
              only
             </em>
             be letter and numbers. To allow (but not require) special characters, you should use something like:
            </p>
            <p>
             <code>
              ^(?=.*[A-Za-z])(?=.*\d).{8,}$
             </code>
             to allow any characters
            </p>
            <p>
             or
            </p>
            <p>
             <code>
              ^(?=.*[A-Za-z])(?=.*\d)[A-Za-z\d$@$!%*#?&amp;]{8,}$
             </code>
             to allow specific special characters
            </p>
            <p>
             Likewise, "minimum eight characters, at least one uppercase letter, one lowercase letter and one number:"
            </p>
            <p>
             <code>
              ^(?=.*[a-z])(?=.*[A-Z])(?=.*\d)[a-zA-Z\d]{8,}$
             </code>
            </p>
            <p>
             meets that minimum requirement, but
             <em>
              only
             </em>
             allows letters and numbers. Use:
            </p>
            <p>
             <code>
              ^(?=.*[a-z])(?=.*[A-Z])(?=.*\d).{8,}$
             </code>
             to allow any characters
            </p>
            <p>
             or
            </p>
            <p>
             <code>
              ^(?=.*[a-z])(?=.*[A-Z])(?=.*\d)[A-Za-z\d$@$!%*?&amp;]{8,}
             </code>
             to allow specific special characters.
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">
            <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">
             <time datetime="2018-04-08T18:21:19" itemprop="dateCreated">
             </time>
             <div class="flex--item mr16" style="flex: 1 1 100px;">
              <div class="js-post-menu pt2" data-post-id="49721224">
               <div class="d-flex gs8 s-anchors s-anchors__muted fw-wrap">
                <div class="flex--item">
                 <a class="js-share-link js-gps-track" data-controller="se-share-sheet" data-gps-track="post.click({ item: 2, priv: 0, post_type: 2 })" data-s-popover-placement="bottom-start" data-se-share-sheet-license-name="CC BY-SA 3.0" data-se-share-sheet-license-url="https%3a%2f%2fcreativecommons.org%2flicenses%2fby-sa%2f3.0%2f" data-se-share-sheet-location="2" data-se-share-sheet-post-type="answer" data-se-share-sheet-social="facebook twitter " data-se-share-sheet-subtitle="" data-se-share-sheet-title="Share a link to this answer" href="/a/49721224" itemprop="url" rel="nofollow" title="Short permalink to this answer">
                  Share
                 </a>
                </div>
                <div class="flex--item">

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="23268629">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="14" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             14
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/23268629/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Import the JavaScript file
             <code>
              jquery.validate.min.js
             </code>
             .
            </p>
            <p>
             You can use this method:
            </p>
            <pre><code>$.validator.addMethod("pwcheck", function (value) {
    return /[\@\#\$\%\^\&amp;\*\(\)\_\+\!]/.test(value) &amp;&amp; /[a-z]/.test(value) &amp;&amp; /[0-9]/.test(value) &amp;&amp; /[A-Z]/.test(value)
});
</code></pre>
            <ol>
             <li>
              At least one upper case English letter
             </li>
             <li>
              At least one lower case English letter
             </li>
             <li>
              At least one digit
             </li>
             <li>
              At least one special character
             </li>
            </ol>
           </div>

        <a name="40136243">
        </a>
        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="40136243" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="19605150" data-position-on-page="10" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="0" data-score="12" id="answer-40136243" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="40136243">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="12" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             12
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/40136243/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Try this one:
            </p>
            <ol>
             <li>
              Minimum six characters
             </li>
             <li>
              At least one uppercase character
             </li>
             <li>
              At least one lowercase character
             </li>
             <li>
              At least one special character
             </li>
            </ol>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Expression:
             </strong>
            </p>
            <pre><code>"/^(?=.*[a-z])(?=.*[A-Z])(?=.*\d)(?=.*[$@$!%*?&amp;.])[A-Za-z\d$@$!%*?&amp;.]{6, 20}/"
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Optional Special Characters:
            </p>
            <ol>
             <li>
              At least one special character
             </li>
             <li>
              At least one number
             </li>
             <li>
              Special characters are optional
             </li>
             <li>
              Minimum six characters and maximum 16 characters
             </li>
            </ol>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Expression:
             </strong>
            </p>
            <pre><code>"/^(?=.*\d)(?=.*[a-zA-Z]).{6,20}$/"
</code></pre>
            <p>
             If the min and max condition is not required then remove
             <code>
              .{6, 16}
             </code>
            </p>
            <ul>
             <li>
              <strong>
               6
              </strong>
              is minimum character limit
             </li>
             <li>
              <strong>
               20
              </strong>
              is maximum character limit
             </li>
             <li>
              <strong>
               ?=
              </strong>
              means match expression
             </li>
            </ul>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">
            <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">
             <time datetime="2016-10-19T15:51:26" itemprop="dateCreated">
             </time>
             <div class="flex--item mr16" style="flex: 1 1 100px;">
              <div class="js-post-menu pt2" data-post-id="40136243">
               <div class="d-flex gs8 s-anchors s-anchors__muted fw-wrap">
                <div class="flex--item">
                 <a class="js-share-link js-gps-track" data-controller="se-share-sheet" data-gps-track="post.click({ item: 2, priv: 0, post_type: 2 })" data-s-popover-placement="bottom-start" data-se-share-sheet-license-name="CC BY-SA 3.0" data-se-share-sheet-license-url="https%3a%2f%2fcreativecommons.org%2flicenses%2fby-sa%2f3.0%2f" data-se-share-sheet-location="2" data-se-share-sheet-post-type="answer" data-se-share-sheet-social="facebook twitter " data-se-share-sheet-subtitle="" data-se-share-sheet-title="Share a link to this answer" href="/a/40136243" itemprop="url" rel="nofollow" title="Short permalink to this answer">
                  Share
                 </a>
                </div>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="62624132" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="19605150" data-position-on-page="11" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="0" data-score="12" id="answer-62624132" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="62624132">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="12" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             12
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/62624132/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             This worked for me:
            </p>
            <pre><code>^(?=.*[0-9])(?=.*[a-z])(?=.*[A-Z])(?=.*[@$!%*?&amp;])([a-zA-Z0-9@$!%*?&amp;]{8,})$
</code></pre>
            <ul>
             <li>
              At least 8 characters long;
             </li>
             <li>
              One lowercase, one uppercase, one number and one special character;
             </li>
             <li>
              No whitespaces.
             </li>
            </ul>
           </div>

        <a name="68612070">
        </a>
        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="68612070" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="19605150" data-position-on-page="12" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="0" data-score="12" id="answer-68612070" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="68612070">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="12" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             12
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/68612070/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             For standard password requirements I found this to be useful:
            </p>
            <ul>
             <li>
              <p>
               At least 1 alphabet
              </p>
             </li>
             <li>
              <p>
               At least 1 digit
              </p>
             </li>
             <li>
              <p>
               Contains no space
              </p>
             </li>
             <li>
              <p>
               Optional special characters e.g. @$!%*#?&amp;^_-
              </p>
             </li>
             <li>
              <p>
               Minimum 8 characters long
              </p>
              <p>
               <code>
                /^(?=.*[A-Za-z])(?=.*\d)[A-Za-z\d@$!%*#?&amp;^_-]{8,}$/
               </code>
              </p>
             </li>
            </ul>
            <p>
             You can also set the upper limit for example {8,32} up to 32 characters long.
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">

             </time>

                 <a class="js-share-link js-gps-track" data-controller="se-share-sheet" data-gps-track="post.click({ item: 2, priv: 0, post_type: 2 })" data-s-popover-placement="bottom-start" data-se-share-sheet-license-name="CC BY-SA 4.0" data-se-share-sheet-license-url="https%3a%2f%2fcreativecommons.org%2flicenses%2fby-sa%2f4.0%2f" data-se-share-sheet-location="2" data-se-share-sheet-post-type="answer" data-se-share-sheet-social="facebook twitter " data-se-share-sheet-subtitle="" data-se-share-sheet-title="Share a link to this answer" href="/a/68612070" itemprop="url" rel="nofollow" title="Short permalink to this answer">
                  Share
                 </a>
                </div>

            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/45791004/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Not directly answering the question, but does it really have to be a regex?
            </p>
            <p>
             I used to do lots of Perl, and got used to solving problems with regexes. However, when they get more complicated with all the look-aheads and other quirks, you need to write dozens of unit tests to kill all those little bugs.
            </p>
            <p>
             Furthermore, a regex is typically a few times slower than an imperative or a functional solution.
            </p>
            <p>
             For example, the following (not very FP) Scala function solves the original question about three times faster than the regex of the most popular answer. What it does is also so clear that you don't need a unit test at all:
            </p>
            <pre><code>def validatePassword(password: String): Boolean = {
  if (password.length &lt; 8)
    return false

  var lower = false
  var upper = false
  var numbers = false
  var special = false

  password.foreach { c =&gt;
    if (c.isDigit)       numbers = true
    else if (c.isLower)  lower = true
    else if (c.isUpper)  upper = true
    else                 special = true
  }

  lower &amp;&amp; upper &amp;&amp; numbers &amp;&amp; special
}
</code></pre>
           </div>

             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             What about considering the following regex solution:
            </p>
            <p>
             <code>
              ^(?=.*[\w])(?=.*[\W])[\w\W]{8,}$
             </code>
            </p>
            <p>
             Which validates the following:
            </p>
            <ol>
             <li>
              At least one lowercase
             </li>
             <li>
              At least one uppercase
             </li>
             <li>
              At least one digit
             </li>
             <li>
              At least one special character
             </li>
             <li>
              At least it should have 8 characters long.
             </li>
            </ol>
            <p>
             Check it out working at the following link
             <a href="https://regex101.com/r/qPmC06/1/" rel="noreferrer">
              https://regex101.com/r/qPmC06/4/
             </a>
            </p>
           </div>

        <a name="69807687">
        </a>
        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="69807687" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="19605150" data-position-on-page="15" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="0" data-score="10" id="answer-69807687" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="69807687">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="10" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             10
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/69807687/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             For a more strict validation where the following is required:
            </p>
            <ol>
             <li>
              At least One Upper Case Character
             </li>
             <li>
              At least one Lower Case character
             </li>
             <li>
              At least one digit
             </li>
             <li>
              At least one symbol/special character @$!%*#?&amp;^_-
             </li>
             <li>
              Minimum 8 characters/digits
             </li>
            </ol>
            <p>
             Regex:
            </p>
            <pre><code>/(?=.*\d)(?=.*[a-z])(?=.*[A-Z])(?=.*[@$!%*#?&amp;^_-]).{8,}/
</code></pre>
            <p>
             I hope it helps someone with a more stringent.
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">
            <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">
             <time datetime="2021-11-02T08:59:18" itemprop="dateCreated">
             </time>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="65339227" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="19605150" data-position-on-page="17" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="0" data-score="5" id="answer-65339227" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="65339227">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="5" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             5
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/65339227/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <pre><code>/^(?=.*[A-Z])(?=.*[a-z])(?=.*[0-9]).*$/
</code></pre>
            <p>
             this the simple way to use it while validate atleast
             <strong>
              1 uppercase 1 lowercase and 1 number
             </strong>
            </p>
            <p>
             and this is the example while I use in express validation
            </p>
            <pre class="lang-js prettyprint-override"><code>check('password')
    .notEmpty()
    .withMessage('Password cannot be null')
    .bail()
    .isLength({ min: 6 })
    .withMessage('Password must be at least 6 characters')
    .bail()
    .matches(/^(?=.*[A-Z])(?=.*[a-z])(?=.*[0-9]).*$/)
    .withMessage(
      'Must have atleast 1 uppercase, 1 lowercase letter and 1 number'
    ),
</code></pre>
           </div>

        <a name="70338667">
        </a>
        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="70338667" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="19605150" data-position-on-page="18" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="0" data-score="5" id="answer-70338667" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="70338667">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="5" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             5
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/70338667/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Another option is to make use of
             <a href="https://www.rexegg.com/regex-style.html#contrast" rel="noreferrer">
              contrast
             </a>
             in the lookahead assertions using a
             <a href="https://www.regular-expressions.info/charclass.html#negated" rel="noreferrer">
              negated character class
             </a>
             , optionally matching any character except that is listed before matching the character that should be matched.
            </p>
            <pre><code>^(?=[^A-Z\n]*[A-Z])(?=[^a-z\n]*[a-z])(?=[^0-9\n]*[0-9])(?=[^#?!@$%^&amp;*\n-]*[#?!@$%^&amp;*-]).{8,}$
</code></pre>
            <p>
             See a
             <a href="https://regex101.com/r/XHHxA5/1" rel="noreferrer">
              regex demo
             </a>
            </p>
            <p>
             In parts, the pattern matches:
            </p>
            <ul>
             <li>
              <code>
               ^
              </code>
              Start of string
             </li>
             <li>
              <code>
               (?=[^A-Z\n]*[A-Z])
              </code>
              Positive lookahead, assert 0+ times any char except A-Z or a newline. Then match a char A-Z
             </li>
             <li>
              <code>
               (?=[^a-z\n]*[a-z])
              </code>
              The same approach for a char a-z
             </li>
             <li>
              <code>
               (?=[^0-9\n]*[0-9])
              </code>
              The same approach for a digit 0-9
             </li>
             <li>
              <code>
               (?=[^#?!@$%^&amp;*\n-]*[#?!@$%^&amp;*-])
              </code>
              The same approach for a char that you would consider special
             </li>
             <li>
              <code>
               .{8,}
              </code>
              Match 8 or more times any character except a newline
             </li>
             <li>
              <code>
               $
              </code>
              End of string
             </li>
            </ul>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Notes
             </strong>
            </p>
            <ul>
             <li>
              A dot can also match a space. If you do not want to allow matching a space, then
              <code>
               .{8,}
              </code>
              can be changed to
              <code>
               \S{8,}
              </code>
              to match 8 or more non whitespace characters
             </li>
             <li>
              Using either
              <code>
               .
              </code>
              or
              <code>
               \S
              </code>
              can match more characters than are specified in the lookahead assertions. If you only want to match the characters that are used in the assertions, you can change
              <code>
               .{8,}
              </code>
              to match only the allowed characters
              <code>
               [#?!@$%^&amp;*A-Za-z0-9-]{8,}
              </code>
              using a character class
             </li>
            </ul>
            <p>
             <div class="snippet" data-babel="false" data-console="true" data-hide="false" data-lang="js">
              <div class="snippet-code">
               <pre class="snippet-code-js lang-js prettyprint-override"><code>const regex = /^(?=[^A-Z\n]*[A-Z])(?=[^a-z\n]*[a-z])(?=[^0-9\n]*[0-9])(?=[^#?!@$%^&amp;*\n-]*[#?!@$%^&amp;*-]).{8,}$/;
[
  "abcA1#!A",
  "#!asdfSFD1;",
  "# a f F1 ;",
  "1111111111",
  "aaaaaaaa",
  "11111111",
  "AAAAAAAA",
  "########",
  "aA1#"
].forEach(s =&gt;
  console.log(regex.test(s) ? `Match --&gt; ${s}` : `No match --&gt; ${s}`)
);</code></pre>
              </div>
             </div>
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">
            <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">

          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Testing this one in 2020:
            </p>
            <pre><code>^(?=.*[a-z])(?=.*[A-Z])(?=.*\d)(?=.*[@$!%*?&amp;])[A-Za-z\d@$!%*?&amp;]{8,}$
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Verify yourself
            </p>
            <p>
             <div class="snippet" data-babel="false" data-console="true" data-hide="false" data-lang="js">
              <div class="snippet-code">
               <pre class="snippet-code-js lang-js prettyprint-override"><code>const regex = /^(?=.*[a-z])(?=.*[A-Z])(?=.*\d)(?=.*[@$!%*?&amp;])[A-Za-z\d@$!%*?&amp;]{8,}$/;
const str = `some12*Nuts`;
let m;

if ((m = regex.exec(str)) !== null) {
    // The result can be accessed through the `m`-variable.
    m.forEach((match, groupIndex) =&gt; {
        console.log(`Found match, group ${groupIndex}: ${match}`);
    });
}</code></pre>
              </div>
             </div>
            </p>
           </div>
